Secondary Flood in Various Counties of Guangdong 73

Eastern River, Shenzhen, Shitanzhen a Vast Expanse of Water

Significant Flood Disaster in Xijiang, Sihui, and Sanshui Guangzhou Dispatch: Since the end of last month, the rains in Guangdong Province have not stopped. Guangzhou City has already suffered a massive flood. In recent days, heavy rains have fallen in various counties, causing the water levels in the East River and West River to rise again. Especially in the downstream areas of the East River and West River, the water cannot be discharged in time, and the counties have been flooded. It has been found that in the area where the East River flows into the sea, near the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway, such as Shenzhen to Shitanzhen, all the rice paddies and houses have been flooded. Old houses have collapsed one after another, and even large trees several fathoms in height have been submerged more than halfway in the water. Looking from a high place, there is only a vast expanse of water. The residents of the disaster area are leading the old and supporting the young, escaping to the province, which is a pitiful sight. As for the West River, the water level from Fengchuan Lianjiangkou to Duchengtang has surged to more than two zhang. Sanshui County, located downstream, bears the brunt of the disaster. The water depth in Hekou Street exceeds seven feet, and small boats are used for transportation on the inner streets. Commerce has completely ceased. Residents of Hekou and Xinan have all fled to Sanshui County to escape the flood. Sihui County, located in the center of the West River, has recently been inundated with rainwater pouring down from Huaiji, Guangxi, making Sihui, a small place, the tail end of the water flow. As a result, most of the county's rice paddies have been flooded, and there is no hope of a harvest this autumn. Seven or eight out of ten houses outside the city have been flooded, and the city has become a watery domain. As for the embankments in various places, those that have been breached by the floodwaters in recent days include the Sanyi Embankment, which has a breach of more than fifty zhang, and the Cangqian Embankment, which has a breach of more than twenty zhang. Not a single tile remains in the villages within the embankments, and the villagers have been displaced. According to a telegram from the Magistrate of Sihui County, since July 31, the county seat has been experiencing continuous rain. Due to the low-lying terrain of the county, the water depth on the streets throughout the city exceeds eight or nine feet. All shops have temporarily suspended business, and the residents are extremely frightened. If one were to climb to the top of Yeli Hill in the county, one would see that all the fields and houses in the county seat area and the surrounding villages have been flooded, creating a vast expanse of water. The sound of gongs and alarms signaling the collapse of embankments in various villages and districts can be heard continuously. This is said to be the greatest disaster the county has experienced in ten years. After receiving the report, the provincial authorities ordered the River Management Association to send personnel to repair the embankments and ordered the Relief Section of the Department of Civil Affairs to allocate funds for relief. (August 9th)

Third Day of Trial in the Noulens Case (Continued) 74

Expert on Handwriting Identification States His Opinion Four Times

Noulens Deliberately Obstructs, Judge Displays Anger At this point, Mei Sheng presented three enlarged photographs, all of which were photographs of applications to the Electric Company for electricity. The judge asked whether the handwriting on these three photographs was the same as that on the letter to the Mei Feng Bank. Mei replied that the main text of these three photographs was not written by Noulens, but the handwriting of the signature and address was the same. He also said that when identifying the handwriting, he used another document as a reference, namely, the letter Noulens sent to the police chief on June 16th of last year. At this time, Noulens requested that the content of this letter be read aloud. Its content was "I now authorize Mr. Fei to collect 1,100 US dollars." Noulens said that it was not stated here that this 1,100 US dollars was mine. Mei Sheng said that the content of this letter did not matter because it was only used to identify the handwriting. Next, the reasons for identifying the handwriting on the three applications were stated as follows: (1) Application for electricity for Room 30, 49 Nanjing Road, C Section, signed Allison. The handwriting on this application is the same as that on the letter to the Mei Feng Bank. The direction of the characters is written to the right, the size of the characters is uneven, the top of the O is also open, the stroke on the left is lower than that on the right, and the handwriting is uneven. Judging from the structure of the characters, the capital A in Allison is exactly the same as the capital A in American on the letter to the Mei Feng Bank. The I is also the same. Also, the mathematical number 04 of 40 on the Mei Feng Bank is exactly the same as the 4 of 49 Nanjing Road. The way of writing the two characters NG is also the same. The stroke of the N is straight down, the lower part of the G is slanted down. Also, the strokes of the two characters RB are the same. Therefore, the handwriting on this application is the same as the handwriting on the letter to the Mei Feng Bank. (2) Application for electricity for 66 Hart Road, signed SHarrisns. The S is larger than the other characters, the same as the S on the letter to the Mei Feng Bank. The capital H is also the same, the way of writing the S is also the same, and the E is also smaller than the previous letter. The way of writing the N is the same as the way of writing it in the letter, so it is determined that the handwriting on this application is the same as the handwriting on the letter to the Mei Feng Bank. (3) Application for electricity for Room 4, 235 Sichuan Road, signed Nulens. The handwriting is the same as the handwriting on the letter to the police chief. The structure of the signature is the same. The way of writing the capital N is the same, but the force of the stroke of the N is heavier at the bottom, and the first curve is longer than the second curve. The top of the O is also open, the left is lower than the right, the three characters ENS are not connected to the L, the way of writing the S is also the same, and the bottom is open, which is the same as on the letter to the Mei Feng Bank.

The judge asked Noulens what he had to say about the reasons for the identification. (Noulens) I request that the judge ask the identifier when these photos were taken. The indictment says that there are more than seventy Chinese documents. The identifier only brought one today, and the evidence on the 18th has nothing to do with the Chinese situation. (Judge) Never mind whether it is relevant or not, you only say whether the identification is correct. (Noulens) Why are there more than seventy pieces of evidence, and the others have not been identified? (Judge) Do not talk nonsense. If you really have no criminal acts, why do you answer there when asked here? (Noulens) I request that the court pay attention to the fact that I said in the letter I wrote to the Mei Feng Bank that I authorized Mr. Fei to collect 400,000, and the money in Box C belongs to me. Here, the words "belongs to me" are present. (Judge) The question now is whether the identification is correct, nothing else matters. (Noulens) No answer. The judge then summoned Wang Delizeng.

(Judge) On March 15th of last year, you went to Room 30, Section C, 49 Nanjing Road, and you left three notes. (The judge presented the notes) (Wang) I request that the court read them to me, and read them loudly. (Judge) You have admitted them in both the Shanghai High Second Branch Court and the Supreme Court. Why do you still need to read them? Isn't this deliberately obstructing? At this point, Wang Delizeng still requested to read them. The judge rejected the request, saying that this was not a study of literature, but an identification of handwriting, so there was no need to read them. He handed them to Wang for personal review. Wang refused, and after a long argument, Wang finally took them for review. After reviewing them, he said that these were French notes, meaning "I have waited until half past twelve. I am now going to see the child and ask the doctor. If there are no changes, I will come again around 2:00 pm." At this time, the judge presented another document, which was a French letter typed in English, with words that Wang had changed. Wang again requested that the full text be read aloud. The judge rejected the request again. After another long argument, the translator read the full text aloud. After reading, Wang said that the Chinese court uses Chinese, so please read it in Chinese. The judge said that you do not understand Chinese, so reading it would be useless. If you want to read it in Chinese, then we will not need a translator in the future. Wang still insisted. The judge then read the four translations and asked if the words he changed were changed by him. Wang did not answer. At this time, Noulens suddenly requested that the English translation be read again. The judge was enraged, saying that he was deliberately obstructing and intentionally disrupting the proceedings. The audience was also angry and impatient. The judge asked Wang Delizeng again, but Wang still did not answer. The judge said that he was hurting himself and ordered the clerk to record it. He ordered Mei Sheng to express his opinion.

(Mei Sheng) This French letter was sent from Singapore on May 27th of last year. I compared it with the handwriting on the notes, and it is the same. There are also two photos here. (1) The O in the two handwritings starts from the lower left and falls down before starting again. (2) Both contain the word Avec. The A starts from the lower left, goes around in a circle, and then writes the location of the bay in the middle of the circle. The A and V are not connected, and the EC is written separately. (3) The way of writing the N is that the second curve is very sharp. (2) The R has two ways of writing, one round is square, and the other is sharp. (5) The format and arrangement of the characters are also exactly the same, so it is determined that they are written by the same person. (Judge) Wang Delizeng, what do you have to say? (Wang) I object to the police officers being used as identifiers. The court previously refused to allow foreign lawyers to appear in court. Why are you now looking for a British identifier? (Judge) This is your misunderstanding. The identifier is based on his knowledge and has nothing to do with the agency. The reason why lawyers cannot appear in court is stipulated by the lawyers' regulations. The identifier is not restricted by nationality. You have any comments on the identifier's opinion, if you do not answer, it is your own loss. (Noulens) Foreign lawyers without the right to jurisdiction can appear in Chinese courts. Although there is no legal provision for this, the Bar Association has expressed its opinion. We wanted to hire a lawyer from Germany to handle the case, but the Chinese embassy refused to issue a passport. (Judge) What is the basis for your statement? (Noulens) Finally, I will submit a letter for review. At this point, the judge summoned Mei Sheng again and asked if there was any other evidence. Mei Sheng expressed his opinion on the identification of the handwriting on the order form for Noulens's custom-made suit at a Western clothing store, but said that this form did not have an enlarged photograph, but the handwriting was indeed the same. The reasons were (1) The Alison signed on the electricity application for 49 Nanjing Road is the same as the Alison signed on this order form. (2) Each character is not connected. (3) The two characters AI are particularly obvious, and the VR are particularly tall. (4) The capital MR is also the same. (5) The two characters ON are also exactly the same. At this point, the judge ordered Mei Sheng to sign and swear again and ordered him to prepare an identification report to be submitted to the court. Mei Sheng said that he could submit it in two or three days. The previously read transcripts and all eight enlarged photographs, six about Noulens and two about Wang Delizeng, were all stored in the case file. The judge ordered the defendants to be taken back into custody and scheduled the court to reconvene for further trial at 1:00 pm on the 15th. The court adjourned in the afternoon.

19th Route Army Attacks Tingzhou in Three Routes 75

Fang Shengtao Goes to Quanzhou to Meet Cai Tingkai

Fuzhou Dispatch: Cai Tingkai, the commander of the 19th Army currently stationed in Zhangzhou, received a telegram from He Yingqin, the commander-in-chief of the bandit suppression in the three provinces of Fujian, Guangdong, and Jiangxi, stating that after Xinfeng was recovered by the Guangdong army, the bandits from the pseudo-First and Fourth Front Armies who had occupied the area had fled to Huichang via Anyuan. The various armies of our bandit suppression are actively taking a surrounding posture and launching a fierce attack. The remnant bandits between Xinfeng and Xingguo will soon be wiped out. However, according to intelligence, Zhu De himself has secretly gone from Huichang to Ruijin. The Red Bandit's pseudo-organization and a large amount of grain and supplies have been moved to that place, which seems to indicate that they intend to flee to Fujian again. You must lead the various units on the front line to quickly cross Liancheng, Longyan, and Shanghang to attack Changting, in order to cut off the bandits' retreat and eliminate the scattered bandits in various places. After receiving the telegram, Commander Cai divided his troops into three routes and ordered Shen Guanghan's unit, currently stationed in Nanjing, to attack the front of Changting via Longyan. Qu Shounian's unit, stationed in Yongding, was ordered to move to Shanghang to attack the left flank of Changting. The newly formed Second Division of Lu Xingbang, stationed in Yong'an, was ordered to attack the right flank of Changting from Liancheng. All were given deadlines for arrival, so that the three routes could launch a general attack simultaneously.

Fang Shengtao, the acting chairman of the provincial government, felt it necessary to discuss the pacification of western and southern Fujian, as well as the defense areas and reorganization issues of the two brigades of Chen Guohui and Chen WeiYuan, currently stationed in Yongchun, Anxi, Putian and Xianyou, with Cai Tingkai in person. On the 2nd, he took a boat to Fuqing with Lin Zhiyuan, a member of the provincial government, and transferred to a long-distance bus via Xinghua to Quanzhou. He also telegraphed Zhangzhou to invite Cai to Quanzhou for talks and to inspect the garrison troops along the way. Fang and Lin arrived in Xianyou on the 4th, where Chen Guohui and Chen Weiyuan both arrived to welcome them and discuss military affairs, waiting for Commander Cai's reply before deciding on their next course of action.

Jiaoji Railway Redemption Plan 76

Jiaoji Railway Bureau Has Drafted a Plan

Past Years' Surplus is Enough to Cover Japanese Debt Qingdao Dispatch: It has been ten years since the Jiaoji Railway was taken over, but the redemption period is only five years away. However, the Chinese people are not prepared for all the redemption matters. When the road was first taken over, the organizers established the Jiaoji Railway Co., Ltd. Preparatory Office, specializing in soliciting shares as a preparation for redemption. At that time, the National Government issued an order to all agencies in Beijing and abroad, deducting 2% of the monthly salary of those with a monthly salary of more than 100 yuan as a redemption savings fund. The handling of the matter could not be said to be lukewarm. Later, due to repeated changes in the political situation and the outbreak of internal wars, the people were unable to even provide for their own livelihoods, and this plan was abolished invisibly. Before long, the Chinese people had become indifferent to this matter. At the end of last month, when the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Inspection Group was in Qingdao, it attached great importance to the issue of redeeming the Jiaoji Railway and had a discussion with the Jiaoji Railway authorities. According to Cui Shijie, a member of the Jiaoji Railway Bureau, the Jiaoji Railway is fully responsible for the redemption issue, but can only contribute opinions for the authorities to adopt. All detailed plans must be jointly planned by the Ministry of Railways and the people of the whole country. There are only five years left until the redemption period. If we do not plan for the repayment early, how can we prevent the Japanese from coveting it? Although the railway's business has been affected by domestic wars over the years, its annual income, in addition to paying Japanese interest, still has a surplus. Although there is no accurate estimate of the railway's assets, the total value is no less than 80 million yuan, which is more than enough to repay the Japanese debt. The railway has drafted two specific plans and submitted them to the Ministry of Railways for review. Before these plans are approved, they cannot be announced due to international credibility. It is hoped that the redemption can be implemented within the time limit to maintain international credit. It is hoped that the Chinese people will work together to make the redemption easier. As for the acquisition of the commercial light railway in Boshan, a request has been submitted to the ministry for instructions. Once the ministry's order arrives, the railway can be taken over. According to another message, the redemption plan drafted by the Jiaoji Railway is (1) The Jiaoji Railway will issue a certain amount of public bonds, with the railway's assets as collateral, as a redemption preparation. (1) Solicit investment from all walks of life, and after the road is redeemed, it will be completely owned by the people. (August 10)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 77

The People's Grand Theater Opens: The entertainment of Songjiang has always been quiet, with only a few bookstores. Now, Xu Kuichen, Zhang Qiyu, and others have organized the People's Grand Theater, which screens movies, and the bus station on the road bridge is used as the theater site. It opened today.

The National Salvation and Anti-Japanese Association Went to Fengjing to Investigate Goods: Xu Zhongming, a standing committee member of the party headquarters, received representatives from the Jiaxing National Salvation and Anti-Japanese Association yesterday, including Huang Tongsheng and Shen Mingcai. They said that the Lunhua Silk and Satin Western Goods Store, which is about to open in Hecheng, had privately imported a large batch of enemy goods, which were loaded onto the Yushunfu ship from Shanghai and delivered to the Hengdachang Western Goods Store in Fengjing to be dyed in preparation for sale. They had come to Fengjing to investigate and requested assistance. Xu, a standing committee member, went to Hengdachang to inquire, but the goods had been transferred to the Lu Tongyuan Dyeing Factory for dyeing. After going to investigate, 110 sections of 84 cloth, fine cloth, and twill were found. The goods were submitted to the Fengjing Anti-Japanese Association for detention. However, Hengdachang said that the cloth was entrusted to them by the Shanghai Jiufu Store and was not imported enemy goods on their behalf. The Jiaxing representatives have returned to Jiaxing to report. It is not known how to negotiate.

National Salvation and Elimination of Traitors Group Established Following the Establishment of the Shanghai Blood Soul Elimination of Traitors Group, a National Salvation and Elimination of Traitors Group was also organized in our county. Yesterday, according to the group's declaration, it stated that Taicang has suffered deeply from the Japanese army since the outbreak of the Shanghai War, and we are extremely resentful of those unscrupulous merchants who are greedy for profit and forget righteousness. Seeing this, we and others have specially organized a National Salvation and Elimination of Traitors Group, which has been formally established. In the future, members will be dispatched to conduct investigations, etc.

Suzhou 79

Discovery of Rice Stem Borers in Dongshan Township Due to the prolonged drought and lack of rain, rice stem borers have been found in the late rice fields in Dongshan Township, but the number is not very large. District Chief Han is afraid of its spread and causing trouble to the area, so he has specially petitioned the county government to find a way to eliminate them. After receiving the report, the county magistrate immediately ordered the Agricultural Improvement Station to quickly send personnel to exterminate them. The Bandit Suppression Department Executes a Lake Bandit After the capture of Shen Liansheng, the pseudo-guerrilla captain under Taihu bandit leader Taibao Ashu, by the First Water Police District, he was handed over to the Suzhou-Songjiang Bandit Suppression Command. After interrogation, Shen Liansheng confessed to robbing merchant ships and resisting enemy officers and soldiers in the Suzhou-Shanghai area. He was sentenced to death and reported to the provincial government for approval. On the morning of the 14th, the prisoner was tied to Wangshudun execution ground and executed by firing squad.

Wuxi 80

The Truth Behind a Bizarre Murder Case is Fully Revealed Wang, the wife of Gu Afu, a villager in Nanqian Village, the 11th district (Nanyan City) of the county, suddenly died in the river while passing through the Sushe Bridge area on the 20th of last month. Subsequently, the family of the deceased accused Zhu Genquan of beating Wang to death and abandoning her body in the river. Zhu Genquan surrendered himself to the authorities. The procuratorate scraped the bones of the corpse for examination, and it was determined that she had died by falling into the river. It is now learned that the case was actually caused by Hua Zhongliang (nicknamed "Touching Wall Ghost"), a local thug in the village. It turned out that when Gu Wang was passing by the door of Zhu Genquan's house in the Sushe Bridge area, she did fall into the river while washing peaches. At that time, Zhu Genquan even went into the river to rescue her, but she died due to excessive water intake and suffocation. After hearing the news, Hua Zhongliang, seeing an opportunity, immediately ordered Zhang Sannan's father, the head of the village, to extort 40 yuan from Zhu. Zhu refused outright because he was unwilling to be wronged. Hua, feeling humiliated, instigated Wang Guanshun, the deceased's brother, to file a petition in court for an autopsy. Now that the truth has been revealed, the procuratorate has telegraphed the Seventh Branch of the Township Public Security Bureau to arrest Hua and bring him to justice. Director Hui of the branch has received the telegram and has arrested Hua to await transfer to the court for interrogation.

A Young Girl Commits Suicide After Being Humiliated The Second District of the County 81

Wu Jiangbo, in Zhangxiang Lane, the villagers Zhang Liangui and his wife usually work outside, leaving only one daughter at home to guard the door. The daughter, named Renxian, is only 18 years old and has excellent looks, but she is of good character and does not indulge in modern habits. She is also diligent in her work, so her parents love her very much. Unexpectedly, A Mao, the daughter of Wang Sangen, suddenly ridiculed Renxian in public the day before yesterday, using veiled language to imply that she had committed adultery, which led to an argument. Wang Sangen and his son Nansheng initially joined in the abuse, and then resorted to violence, severely beating Renxian. After being beaten, Renxian went to her grandmother's house to complain because her parents were out, but her grandmother was bedridden and unable to speak out for her niece. In anger, Renxian felt that she had no one to turn to and hanged herself in secret at 5 p.m. that day. By the time she was discovered, she had already passed away. After hearing the news, Liangui and his wife rushed back overnight and mourned over the body. They have now come to the city to report to the county court for an autopsy.

Changzhou 82

Various Townships in the Third District Report Famine This Spring in Wu County, rain has been a disaster, and after entering summer, there has been a prolonged drought with no rain for two months, causing ditches and ponds to dry up, the land to crack, and the rice seedlings to wither. The autumn harvest has been declared hopeless. In the past two or three days, more than ten townships and towns in the Third District, including Dongqiu, Shiwan, Anning, Lucheng, and Anjiashe, have reported famine to the county and requested that personnel be sent to inspect the situation and find ways to provide relief. Furthermore, there was a slight rainfall the day before yesterday. According to the farmers, the lower-lying fields can still be salvaged, but the higher-lying fields are like pouring a cup of water on a cart of burning firewood, which is still of no avail. Reactionary Criminals Sent to the High Court for Interrogation Zhang Zi'an and Huang Xuezhou, the criminals involved in the reactionary fraud case in Donghenglin, Wu County, surrendered to the Procuratorate of the Court at about 8 a.m. on the 13th for interrogation. After a court hearing, at about 12 p.m., Chief Prosecutor Yang sent police to escort the entire file, along with the two criminals and three other accomplices in custody, including Huang Sheng, to the Suzhou High Court for interrogation.

It was decided that we should resist with conscience and pay extra attention. The request to send personnel for inspection should be unnecessary. (2) This Chamber has heard that enemy goods from Shanghai are being secretly transported inland. This Chamber severely warns all merchants to unanimously refuse to sell them. Furthermore, the Silk and Cloth Trade Association stated that Yuchangxiang and Yongtaichang have become wary since receiving warnings from the Blood Soul Group. On the 12th, the association held a meeting to inform all colleagues that they should be determined never to import enemy goods again. If private imports are discovered, they will be severely punished.

Nantong 84

County Issues Tax-Backed Loan Certificates Worth 100,000 Yuan Due to Nantong's local financial difficulties, the county government, in order to alleviate the urgent situation, proposed to the county administrative meeting to issue county tax-backed loan certificates, following the example of the provincial government's method of issuing grain transport loan certificates. On the 13th, it was resolved to issue a total of 100,000 yuan, which will not be circulated in the same way as the loan certificates issued by the Property Management Office. The face value of the certificates will be divided into 10 yuan and 50 yuan.

Eastern Township Bandit Returned to Military Law for Interrogation The Nantong County Government arrested Pan Lanfang, a bandit from Eastern Township, who confessed to arson, robbery, and murder. He was sentenced to death and reported to the provincial government for approval. The provincial government reviewed the case and determined that the bandit was a deserter and should be returned to the military for interrogation in accordance with military law.

Huzhou 85

Yu Dabianzi Shot Dead While Attempting to Escape Yu Dabianzi, a notorious bandit, committed numerous crimes of kidnapping and looting in the six counties of Huzhou and had been wanted by the provincial government. In June of this year, he was arrested by the Seventh Company of the Security Team stationed in Lijiaxiang at Tiger Cave and sent to the Second Regiment Headquarters in this city for investigation. Because Yu confessed that he had many accomplices hiding near Lijiaxiang, Weixing, and was willing to lead the capture, the regiment headquarters ordered Lu, the company commander of the Seventh Company, to send a team to take Yu back by Huzhou-Changxing bus on the 11th of this month. They stayed temporarily at the company headquarters. At about 4 a.m. the next morning, just as they were about to set off to capture the bandits, Yu suddenly tried to escape. Company Commander Lu immediately ordered the soldiers to shoot Yu dead. He also reported the circumstances to the regiment headquarters for approval.

Shaoxing 86

Major Robbery Occurs Outside Jiskan Gate Shengkang Money Shop in Shaoxing Xinhe Lane had 25,000 yuan in banknotes, which were sent to Hangzhou by Wang on the 12th to withdraw from Yingfeng Money Shop. He carried the money with him. The robbers learned of this and followed him. When they arrived at Xixing, they pulled out a pistol and asked Wang if he was returning to Shaoxing. Wang replied that he was returning to Shaoxing by bus. The robbers said that they also needed to go to Shaoxing and forced him to hire a boat to return to Shaoxing together. When they arrived outside Jishan Gate, the robbers ordered the boat to stop, robbed Wang of 25,000 yuan in banknotes, and went ashore towards Yuling. Before leaving, they fired a pistol at Wang's calf, saying that he could use it for disaster relief. The money shop has reported the incident to the Public Security Bureau and requested them to pursue the robbers. Wang has been sent to the hospital for treatment.

Xiaoshan 87

Suicide Due to Economic Oppression Lu Jingchu, a resident of Zhao Jiawu, a place in the southern countryside of Xiaoshan, was formerly a foreman at a silk mill in Shanghai. Since the Shanghai war this spring, the silk mill has been closed due to the impact, and he lost his job and returned home. Starting last month, his wife fell ill and his son died, making a living difficult. This time, he himself contracted typhoid fever and had no money for treatment, so he cut his throat with a razor to commit suicide in the middle of the night on the 12th. When the neighbors heard the sound and went to rescue him, his throat had already been severed, and he died on the spot.

Bandits Rob in Broad Daylight at Sheqian on the Border of Shaoxing and Xiaoshan There is a place called Sheqian on the border of Xiaoshan and Linpu Yiqiao. There are people of good and bad character traveling on the road every day. On the afternoon of the 11th, two cloth peddlers were stopped by five bandits speaking with mixed accents, who robbed them of 20 yuan in silver dollars and 35 cents in small silver coins. Unexpectedly, on the morning of the 12th, two bandits on the main road from Sheqian to Xiaoshan also stopped a dried bamboo shoot peddler and robbed him of all his possessions: five silver dollars and more than ten cents in small silver coins.

Education News

Special Feature 88

Opinions on the National Sports Conference (3) Lu Pei (9) "Promote universal sports, not only focus on athlete competitions, but also stipulate standard scores and promulgate physical education performance examination methods." The purpose of physical education is not to serve a very small number of outstanding talents, but to promote the health of everyone, indirectly improve their intelligence and morality, and assist their academic studies and the progress of their productivity. In addition to athlete competitions, group competitions should be added. For students of a certain level and age, gender should also be differentiated to stipulate a passing standard, so that the results can be made public, and they can also test themselves, arousing their psychology of practicing at any time and striving upward.

(10) "Stipulate the qualifications of amateur athletes." The qualifications of amateur athletes and the standard and performance examination methods in the previous article have never been fixed, or the results of the students of this school are accommodated to ensure that they all pass, or the methods of foreign countries are adopted too objectively. In my humble opinion, it seems better to change the word "amateur" to "voluntary," and use the qualifications of amateur athletes of the Hong Kong ball club as a blueprint and slightly modify it.

(11) (1) Add two hours of physical theory per week to all levels of normal schools. The content includes the principles of physical education, administrative management, and physical examination methods. A physical education teacher must have the perseverance of a soldier, the attitude of an educator, the responsibility of a doctor, the mind of an engineer, and the heart of a loving mother. If they know what is happening but do not know why, and blindly imitate new things, they will become physical education craftsmen. Therefore, they must study physical education subjects and be familiar with various methods of organization, facilities, guidance, encouragement, training, and testing in order to avoid being ridiculed as physical education craftsmen. (11) (2) "Physical education funds for secondary and higher schools should be independent." When preparing budgets, all secondary schools should separate the physical education fees and the physical education fees collected from students and not use them for other purposes. The physical education director should plan the phased additions, repairs, and distribution of various competitions and sports meets.

(11) (3) "Secondary school students are strictly prohibited from getting married." The Ministry of Education should strictly order all secondary schools to suspend students who have the above situation, regardless of the reason, and not issue transfer certificates. It is best for the Ministry of Interior to order all public security bureaus to require all marriages to be registered a few days in advance and require a doctor's certificate to prove that the body is fully developed, and a lawyer's certificate to prove their true age, name, address, and occupation in order to have legal effect.

(11) (4) The traditional class system should be abolished for physical education training. Physical education training should be divided into physical fitness, physical energy, and physical strength, and should vary according to age and gender. It seems inappropriate to use male rules for women's sports. In addition to group general training, special training should also be added to correct defects and promote balanced development. If the standard is based on the level of Chinese, English, arithmetic, etc., it will be like scratching an itch from outside a boot, and there will never be universal and balanced development.

(11) (5) Strictly prohibit women from wearing strange and enchanting clothes that hinder their physiology. Women are strictly prohibited from wearing corsets, perming their hair, wearing stiff collars, shoes with too high heels, and all clothing that is unhygienic and harmful to public morals. Female students should all wear short clothes and short skirts at school. However, this article cannot rely solely on official documents and should be vigorously promoted by the education community and lead by example to achieve complementary results. On the one hand, the Ministry of Interior should order local administrative and public security agencies to strictly stipulate punishment regulations. (11) (6) Increase the salary of physical education teachers. The salary of the physical education director should be equal to that of the academic affairs director. Physical education teachers should be treated the same as other liberal arts teachers. Now, not all schools in Jiangsu Province are uniform, and some physical education class hours have not been followed as stipulated by the Ministry, which should be corrected. Those who are old and have made considerable achievements should be given retirement benefits. Those who become disabled due to official duties should be given pensions or consolation money. Those who want to study abroad or focus on research to seek further studies or have inventions should be given bonuses. (11) (7) All schools should uniformly add a physical education director. Except for students under 100, there should be one physical education director and several teachers or instructors to manage all physical education matters in the school. To achieve the purpose of Article 14 above, a physical education director is even more indispensable. If so, the school sports field should be large and have more equipment, and teachers must also be increased. Although the cost is higher, the benefits to education and school spirit are great and definitely not a waste. Moreover, even if there are many teachers, the school expenses can also be saved by having them concurrently serve as life guidance or administrative duties. (End)

The 3rd Rotary Cup Chinese Retained Championship 90

Retained for the Third Time Double won by Chinese with a Clean Sweep of Three Games Another Two Singles Groups Canceled The third Rotary Cup International Tennis Tournament, which caused a sensation in the entire city, saw the Chinese team defeat Portugal in the first battle and then defeat Britain in the final, thus retaining the championship for the third consecutive year. Today, there are still two singles groups between China and Britain, but because the championship has been decided, the competition has been canceled.

Chinese Team Reigns Supreme for Three Years 91

The Rotary Cup began in 1930 and was donated by the Shanghai Rotary Club to be hosted by the China National Sports Association for the Shanghai International Tennis Championship. For a time, people came from all directions, and the wind and clouds stirred. The championship for the first and second years was won by China. This is the third year, and China is once again seen continuing to reign supreme, which is enough to be called worthy.

Draft National Physical Education Implementation Plan (2) 98

As for the local administration, there is no uniform method in the education halls and bureaus of each province and city. Some have physical education instructors, some have public sports field directors, some have physical education committees, and recently some have physical education supervisors. Even those without physical education administrative organizations are still in the majority. Since the titles of administrative personnel are not the same, the duties they perform are also inconsistent, making it difficult to achieve common goals. As for those local administrative agencies that have no physical education administrative organization, it can be seen that they do not fundamentally seek the development of physical education. Therefore, it is difficult to standardize.

Education Hall 99

In order to ensure administrative organization and actual administrative effectiveness, the education halls and bureaus of each province and city should set up at least one physical education supervisor to study, inspect, and urge the implementation of physical education. Whether to set up a physical education committee should be considered based on the local situation. The original public sports field directors will still remain in their posts. Those without public sports fields should find ways to add them. The committee and supervisor system in Hebei Province and the public sports field system in Shandong and Jiangsu Provinces can all be adopted by other provinces. The organization of the education halls and bureaus in each province and city is different. Here is a system table based on the general halls and bureaus:

As for the duties of the supervisor, in addition to inspecting and guiding the physical education of schools at all levels, he should perform the following duties: (1) Formulate the physical education plan for the entire province (2) Prepare the physical education administrative budget for the entire province (3) Review the physical education budgets of all schools in the province (4) Stipulate the detailed physical education curriculum for the entire province and urge its experimentation and implementation (5) Review physical education organizations that request registration and filing (6) Study and improve the methods of physical education in the entire province (7) Handle physical education performance evaluation matters for the entire province. At present, the physical education situation in each province is mostly simple and crude, and each has its own special circumstances and difficulties. The steps of the physical education supervisor's work must be scientific, starting from investigating and inspecting the actual situation in various places, and then formulating the goals and plans for implementation gradually. It is absolutely forbidden to act rashly and mislead people, and it is even more forbidden to have no plan, changing orders in the morning and evening, causing those who are responsible for physical education to be at a loss.

(2) Equipment 100

The economic situation in our country is so low, and the physical education equipment of schools at all levels and public sports is extremely simple and crude. It is extremely difficult to seek appropriate equipment. The equipment standards set this time are actually the lowest standards from the perspective of physical education. However, in terms of national conditions, it seems too idealistic. However, if we want to develop physical education, poor equipment is the biggest obstacle. If those who preside over education administration can understand the importance of physical education and the necessity of its equipment and strive to expand it, it may not be impossible. Therefore, it is better to focus on ideals as the goal of efforts in the education and sports communities, rather than being too accommodating to reality and making physical education equipment equal to zero. The equipment that each level of school and public sports field should have is listed below. The above-listed fields are the minimum for elementary schools with less than 100 students. For elementary schools with more than 100 students, each 100 students should be doubled, and those with less than 50 students can be added by half. Elementary schools that only have lower grades and rural elementary schools that cannot prepare fields according to the above principles under special circumstances should use 100 square feet of playground space for each student as the minimum standard. (2) Fixed Equipment Organ or gramophone One Horizontal bar Two Giant steps One Swing One Slide One Seesaw One High jump stand (can be used as a jump rope stand) Two pairs Basketball hoop Two pairs (one pair for men and one pair for women) Volleyball net One pair or two pairs Mats (approximately 150 square feet) Two The above-listed fixed equipment is the minimum for elementary schools with less than 100 students. For elementary schools with more than 100 students, each 100 students should be doubled, and those with less than 50 students can be added by half. (3) Consumable Equipment Basketball net Two pairs Volleyball net Two Ball bats Four Ball paddles Two pairs Basketball Three Volleyball Three Ball Six Ball Two Medicine balls Four (Weight must be increased) Lime Two hundred catties Air pump Two Thin rope Four hundred feet Lime line drawing pot Two The above-listed consumable equipment is the minimum standard for each semester for elementary schools with less than 100 students. For elementary schools with more than 100 students, each 100 students should be doubled, and those with less than 50 students can be added by half.

National Sports Conference to Open Tomorrow 101

(1) Members Register One After Another The National Sports Conference will be held at the Lizhi Society on Huangpu Road, Nanjing, starting on the morning of the 16th. Members will be accommodated at the Lizhi Society. Members can move in on the morning of the 16th. The Ministry of Education will set up a registration office in the Ministry of Education's meeting room from 8:00 a.m. on the 13th to 5:00 p.m. on the 15th. The registration procedures include submitting proof of identity, filling out the registration book, reviewing the meeting identification group (according to the rules for reviewing proposals, tentatively (1) school sports, (2) public sports, (3) children's sports, (4) women's sports, (5) national arts, (6) physical education administration, (7) other, etc., seven groups. Each person is limited to recognizing two groups), and collecting identification cards, handbooks, accommodation certificates, etc.

(2) Distinguishing the Participants 102

The participants in this conference are: 1. School sports directors, 2. Provincial and municipal sports representatives, 3. Principals of physical education colleges, 4. Directors of national arts halls, 5. Sports experts, 6. Representatives of agencies, 7. Responsible officials (Ministry of Education). The 13th was the first day of registration for the conference, and the number of registered people was not large. The number of participating members and the number of proposals submitted by the 12th have been recorded in the newspapers. On the 13th, the Hong Kong Sports Association telegraphed that it would send Zhao Qianghua to attend. Several other proposals have also been submitted. The association, after checking the provisions of Article 2, Item 7 of the conference regulations (one councilor should be added to attend after the regulations are revised), has already requested the Ministry of Education to appoint Councilor Yang Fang as a member of the National Sports Conference on the 13th (the revised text of Article 2, Item 7 of the regulations is the Minister, Vice Minister, and one Councilor of the Ministry of Education, as well as the directors and section chiefs of each responsible department).

(3) The Staff of the Conference 103

In addition, there are more than 20 people from the Ministry of Education's secretariat, section chiefs, and section members who are serving as conference staff (Conference secretaries Wu Yan, Zhong Lingxiu, Daily Editor-in-Chief Yi Keyi, General Manager Guo Lianfeng, Document Section staff Gu Wenjie, Weng Zhida, Huang Longxian, Gao Hongtu, Huang Wenqi, Jin Guisun, Wang Gen, He Boli, Wang, Reception Section staff Shi Wei, Zhang Yuanxun, Tu Gang, Dai Ce fan, Jia Guoren, Xie Zhuozi, Shu Chushi, Wei Xuezhi, Zhu Shusen, Zou Fengji). A letter was sent to the Ministry of Finance requesting that it select and send a representative to attend, and it was hoped that the representative's name and resume would be sent to the meeting in advance.

(4) Proposal Group Review Undetermined 104

The classification of proposals (previously divided into twenty categories) and the issue of group review (seven groups) have not yet been fully determined. For example, in grouping, if we consider the first school sports organization from the vertical perspective of the educational system, the so-called university, middle school, and primary school can be consistent. However, from the horizontal perspective, there are differences in school sports facilities, curriculum materials, teachers, etc., which must be studied separately. Whether the future approach will be to have each major group include several categories for combined review, or to add more groups because the seven groups cannot be summarized, will depend on the discussion at the general meeting.

The Record of Knocking on the Bell in the Old Temple is Not to Remove the Court Grass (74) 117

Mr. Tang said, "Even so, your production is too slow compared to modern machine production and will eventually be eliminated. If you want not to be eliminated, you must adopt Fordism - 'one person, one action'." Mr. Zhu said, "Why be fast? Because production is faster than people, and prices are cheaper than people, you can seize the market from people. This is purely the expression of individual competition in machine construction. If you want production to be faster and faster, you must divide the work finer and finer until you reach 'one person, one action'. I think reversing Ford's words would better describe his spirit. The result of Fordism is 'one action, one person'. One person, all day long, all year round, all their life doing this one monotonous action. If they don't end up half-dead, they will inevitably develop mental illness. So, Fordism begins with one person doing one action and ends with one action destroying one person. It turns good people into lunatics and the world into hell. You ask Ford himself to work in a car factory according to the 'one person, one action' method for a year and a half. See if he is willing to do it again, see if he is willing to call his children to do it, and see if he is still willing to implement this 'one person, one action' principle." Mr. Tang said, "You seem to be against machines, don't you?" Mr. Zhu said, "I am not against machines, but I think our concept of machines needs a fundamental change. The predecessors who made machines put all their eyes on production! The faster and more the production, the better the machine can be considered perfect. He completely ignored the workers who used the machines. In the future, scientific inventions of machines should shift their gaze to the workers. We want to create machines for people, not machines for slaves - we want to create machines that benefit people, not machines that harm people - we want to create machines that nourish people, not machines that destroy people. Our purpose is to create all kinds of machines so that the people who use them can enjoy their work. In the future world, only this new machine with human life at its center can exist. All machines that enslave, harm, and destroy people must be smashed to pieces and placed in the stove to recreate that new machine with human life at its center. This new machine with human life at its center has no extravagant hope; it does not want to turn the world into paradise; it will not turn the world into hell; its mission is to turn an unreasonable world into a reasonable human world. This is the new machine doctrine we want to realize."

Wu Zhihui Flew to Shanghai from Hankou Yesterday. Key Figures Met with Wang Jingwei 118

Wang's Resignation is Firm, but He Has Agreed to Go to Beijing Within Days

He, Wu, Zhu, and Others Returned to Beijing by Night Train Last Night to Report

Wang and Zhang Decided to Go Together and Will Discuss Successor Candidates

The Political Situation Took a Sharp Turn and Can Be Fully Resolved This Week

Regarding the resignation of Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan, due to the ineffectiveness of continuous retention efforts from various parties, the political situation is extremely somber. The central government previously sent Central Committee member Wu Zhihui to Hankou to discuss everything with Chiang Kai-shek. Yesterday afternoon at 3 o'clock, Mr. Wu arrived in Shanghai by plane from Hankou and immediately went to visit Song Ziwen and others to exchange opinions. He then wired Wang's residence and arranged a meeting with Wang. Yesterday afternoon at 5 o'clock, Wu Zhihui, Song Ziwen, He Yingqin, Zhu Peide, Zhu Jiahua, and others went to Wang's residence on Pushi Road. Wang was already there as agreed. The two sides talked for more than an hour before Wu, Song, He, and others excused themselves and left. According to He Yingqin, after three meetings with Wang, he had achieved satisfactory results. Wang had agreed to return to Beijing within days, and the political situation could be restored to stability. Last night at 11 o'clock, He Yingqin, Wu Zhihui, Zhu Peide, Zhu Jiahua, Zeng Zhongming, and others took the night train back to Beijing to report the results of their negotiations in Shanghai to the central government. According to Zeng Zhongming, Wang and Zhang resigned together, and the central government will approve both. Currently, only the issue of successor candidates remains. In any case, it can be fully resolved by the middle of next week. The political situation has taken a sharp turn for the better. The details are recorded separately as follows:

Wu Arrived in Shanghai by Plane 119

Mr. Wu Zhihui of the central government previously went to Hankou from Beijing to visit Chiang Kai-shek to discuss the solution to the political situation. He has now achieved considerable results and arrived in Shanghai by plane from Hankou at 3 PM yesterday. After disembarking, he immediately went to Song's residence on Qi Qi Road to visit Song Ziwen and report Chiang's views. Soon after, Zhu Peide, He Yingqin, and Zhu Jiahua arrived at Song's residence one after another and discussed with Mr. Wu for a long time. They then wired Wang's residence and arranged a meeting with Wang. Wang agreed to wait at his residence at 5 o'clock.

The Final Meeting at Wang's Residence 120

Yesterday afternoon at 5 o'clock, Wu Zhihui, Song Ziwen, He Yingqin, Zhu Peide, Zhu Jiahua, and others went to Wang's residence on Pushi Road. Wang Jingwei personally received them. First, Wu stated Chiang's intentions, still hoping that Wang would return to Beijing soon to resume his duties. As for Zhang Xueliang's resignation, the central government decided to approve it. Wang immediately stated that he would never return to the position of President of the Executive Yuan, but he would work hard at other positions. Then, Song, He, Zhu, and others repeatedly persuaded him, but Wang finally refused. As a result, Song, He, and others drafted a compromise plan, asking Wang to return to Beijing within days to stabilize the political situation. At the same time, the central government would approve his resignation and appoint him to another important position. Only then did Wang agree. The meeting lasted for an hour and a half.

He and Wu Returned to Beijing Together 121

He Yingqin, Wu Zhihui, Zhu Peide, Zhu Jiahua, and others, believing that there had been considerable results in persuading Wang, took the night train back to Beijing at 11 o'clock last night to attend this morning's Central Standing Committee discussion meeting to report the results of their negotiations in Shanghai and discuss Zhang Xueliang's resignation. According to the Central News Agency, today's Central Standing Committee discussion meeting will be changed to a standing committee meeting to make a resolution on the resignation of Zhang Xueliang, the Director of the Peiping Pacification Headquarters.

Although colleagues have not yet been able to dispel President Wang's intention to resign, President Wang values national affairs and has agreed to go to Beijing within days. Investigation into the Fineness of Silver Coins by Expert Edward Kann 133

Most groups advocate following the Third Year of the Republic Regulations.

However, the Third Year of the Republic Regulations were not effectively implemented. This time, the Central Bank convened a committee to study the abolition of taels and the adoption of the yuan. Based on the proposal of expert Edward Kann, the weight of the new coin was set at 7 qian and 9 li, and the fineness at 88% silver and 12% copper. This has been largely resolved and is pending official approval from the Ministry of Finance. Mr. Kann has been engaged in the financial sector in China for over twenty years and has conducted in-depth research on Chinese currency. His proposals are based on detailed and meticulous investigations. According to sources obtained by the New Voice Society, the basis of his investigations is as follows:

The Fineness of Old Coins from the Late Qing Dynasty 134

Since the Guangdong Provincial Mint began casting dragon dollars in the fifteenth year of the Guangxu reign, marking the start of China's own production of silver coins, various provinces successively followed suit. According to an investigation in the eighth year of the Republic, the total amount of old coins cast by various Chinese mints was 286,351,413 yuan. Their weight and fineness are as follows: (1) Guangdong: weight 7.245 Kuping taels, each yuan contains 6.540 taels of silver, fineness 899.60; (2) Hubei: weight 7.226, contains 6.530 taels of silver, fineness 900.10; (3) Jiangnan: weight 7.243, contains 6.538 taels of silver, fineness 899.50; (4) Beiyang Machine Bureau: weight 7.289, contains 6.386 taels of silver, fineness 890.00; (5) Beiyang Branch: weight 7.396, contains 6.582 taels of silver, fineness 888.90; (6) Fengtian Machine Bureau: weight 7.247, contains 6.207 taels of silver, fineness 843.50; (7) Fengtian Branch: weight 7.074, contains 5.959 taels of silver, fineness 843.50; (8) Eastern Three Provinces: weight 7.191, contains 6.400 taels of silver, fineness 889.50; (9) Jilin: weight 6.9880, contains 6.178 taels of silver, fineness 889.40; (10) Sichuan: weight 7.179, contains 6.437 taels of silver, fineness 886.80; (11) Anhui: weight 7.229, contains 6.477 taels of silver, fineness 887.20; (12) General Mint: weight 7.209, contains 6.521 taels of silver, fineness 900.30. In the second year of the Xuantong reign, the government was requested to issue a national currency law stipulating that the new currency unit be the yuan, commonly known as the Daqing silver coin. The master mold for this coin was cast by the Tianjin Mint and submitted to the Qing court for approval. Its weight was 7 qian and 2 fen Kuping taels, and its fineness was 900. From the third year of Xuantong, the Wuchang and Nanjing Mints began trial casting, expecting it to circulate in the winter of that year. However, the Wuchang Uprising occurred in October, and in a hurry, mostly mixed coins were used to pay salaries. Several years later, the Sichuan military government issued a new type of coin called the Dahan silver coin, which was one of the last types of currency of the Qing Dynasty.

The Third Year of the Republic Regulations Were Not Effectively Implemented 135

Currently, commercial organizations in various provinces and cities advocate that the weight and fineness of future new silver coins should comply with the National Currency Regulations of the Third Year of the Republic. These regulations stipulated that the fineness should be 900/1000, weighing 7 qian and 2 fen Kuping taels, meaning that the pure silver content should weigh 6 qian and 4 fen and 8 li Kuping taels. In reality, these regulations were never effectively implemented. The casting of Yuan Shikai coins was closely related to the recall and recasting of 280 million yuan of dragon dollars at that time. The fineness of the dragon dollars was lower than that stipulated. If those with lower fineness were recast into those with higher fineness, the government would inevitably suffer losses. At that time, the treasury was in dire straits and unable to bear this loss, so it had to reduce the fineness of the Yuan Shikai coins to 890/1000. However, according to statistics from A. Tracey Woodward, the fineness of Yuan Shikai coins was as follows: (1) Coins from the Third Year of the Republic: weight 414.73 British grains, fineness 880; (2) Coins from the Eighth Year of the Republic: weight 413.37 British grains, fineness 880; (3) Coins from the Ninth Year of the Republic: weight 413.99 British grains, fineness 880; (4) Coins from the Tenth Year of the Republic: weight 414.66, fineness 880. By the thirteenth year of the Republic, the highest fineness of inferior Yuan Shikai coins discovered in the Anhui Mint and in Shanghai in the fourteenth year of the Republic was 823, and the lowest was only 744. Therefore, it is most appropriate and feasible to stipulate the fineness of new coins at 880, as stipulating it too high would inevitably repeat the failure of the Third Year of the Republic Regulations.

Names of Mints in Various Provinces 136

According to Edward Kann's plan for the abolition of taels and adoption of the yuan, the biggest prerequisite is to ensure that the fineness, weight, form, and area of silver dollars across the country are completely uniform. Casting must be concentrated in one agency, so that all silver dollars in the country are exclusively made by the designated mint, which is currently the Central Mint in Shanghai. The locations of the mints in various provinces are as follows: (1) Nanjing Mint; (2) Qingjiangpu Mint, specializing in copper coins; (3) Hangzhou Mint, already closed; (4) Anqing Mint; (5) Fuzhou Mint; (6) Fujian Hongshanqiao Mint; (7) Fujian Mehe Mint; (8) Shaxian Mint; (9) Xiamen Mint; (10) Guangxi Nanning Mint; (11) Guangxi Wuzhou Mint; (12) Guilin Mint; (13) Guangzhou Mint; (14) Yunnan Mint; (15) Wuchang Mint; (16) Nanchang Mint; (17) Changsha Mint; (18) Chengdu Mint; (19) Chongqing Mint; (20) Xi'an Mint; (21) Lanzhou Mint; (22) Taiyuan Mint; (23) Jinan Mint; (24) Tianjin Mint; (25) Beiyang Mint; (26) Zhangjiakou Mint; (27) Shenyang Mint; (28) Jilin Mint; (29) Dihua Mint. The circumstances of the above mints, whether specializing in copper coins, silver coins, or both, varied, and most of them have already ceased casting.

The Shanghai Standard Silver Unit 137

The Shanghai business community's change in the unit of account to the Shanghai Kuping Tael, namely 98 Kuping Silver, started in the sixth year of Xianfeng, i.e., 1856. Before the sixth year of Xianfeng, the 'Benyang' (foreign dollar) was practically the only circulating silver coin in China, its influence spreading to Guangdong, Fujian, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and other provinces. Exchange rates quoted by banks were also based on this. However, around the twentieth year of Daoguang, the minting of Benyang stopped, and the source gradually dried up. Soon, its price in various provinces and cities gradually increased, exceeding its silver value by about 20-30%. As a result, business was severely hampered. Therefore, the Shanghai business community changed the unit of account to the Shanghai Kuping Tael. It is said that in that year, when various Shanghai banks and commercial organizations switched to using the Shanghai Kuping Tael, the market price of Benyang happened to be equal to the Shanghai Kuping Tael. Therefore, only the unit name needed to be changed on the account books, while the numbers could remain the same. This is also an interesting story. Currently, the Benyang is no longer a circulating currency in China.

Edward Kann's Theory of Chinese Currency 138

Edward Kann, drawing on his experience of over twenty years in the banking business in major commercial ports in China, wrote a book entitled "Theory of Chinese Currency," divided into three sections: gold, silver, and copper, with extremely detailed discussions. The book was translated by Cai Shoubai of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank and published by the Commercial Press, serving as the most complete reference book for studying Chinese currency systems and exchange rates.

Kim Koo Has Been Arrested 139

Japanese Army and Police Cooperate in the Capture

Currently Detained at the Japanese Consulate General. According to reliable foreign sources, Korean revolutionary leader Kim Koo has been captured by the Japanese Navy in collaboration with Chinese police on Chongming Island and is currently detained at the Japanese Consulate General. Kim Koo's arrest took place several weeks ago. This newspaper's reporter heard about it earlier, but it has only now been confirmed from various sources. Kim Koo is the leader of the Korean independence movement. Since the bombing at Hongkou Park at the end of April, he has been even more closely watched by the Japanese military and political authorities. Later, Kim Koo, fearing the Japanese authorities' intense manhunt, left Shanghai and temporarily sought refuge in the countryside of Chongming. However, his hiding place was also discovered by the Japanese. Japanese Consul General Murai immediately notified the Chinese authorities, requesting cooperation in the capture. Japanese warships approached the vicinity of Chongming, and several marines were dispatched to land, working with local police, using swift and decisive methods to capture Kim Koo and escort him to the Japanese Consulate General for interrogation.

Agreement on the Special District Court Nearing the End of Its Three-Year Term 140

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Decides to Modify the Notification

Negotiations on the Shanghai International Settlement District Court Agreement will commence at the end of this year. The agreement is set to expire on March 31 of next year. The government believes that the content of the agreement is not fully autonomous and has decided to conduct revisions with the relevant countries. Details of the news are as follows:

Notification to Six Countries 141

The court agreement will expire on March 31 of next year (1933). According to personnel of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs stationed in Shanghai, the procedures on the part of the Ministry of Judicial Administration have been prepared after Minister Luo's inspection in Shanghai. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs does not have much procedure, only drafting notifications and preparing to send personnel for negotiation. Currently, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has prepared to notify relevant countries shortly, requesting them to send representatives to conduct negotiations. This negotiation must begin at the end of this year. The countries to be notified include Britain, the United States, France, the Netherlands, Norway, and Brazil, following the old precedent of notifying them separately.

Points for Revision 142

Regarding the points that should be revised in the subsequent negotiations, the principle is to strive to transform it into a judicial institution that is fully autonomous to our country. However, the key points are no more than (1) execution; (2) appointment and dismissal of judicial police; (3) appearance of foreign lawyers in court. According to the provision in the last section of Article 6 of the agreement regarding the power of appointment and dismissal, "The judicial police officers of the said courts shall be appointed by the President of the High Sub-Court after recommendation by the Municipal Council. The President of the High Court shall have the power to dismiss them for stated reasons, or the Municipal Council may terminate their employment with stated reasons." In addition, the section regarding consideration of the Yangjingbang Regulations stipulated in Article 2 of the agreement may also need to be revised.

History of the Agreement 143

The establishment of the Shanghai International Settlement Special District Court Agreement was a modification of the Provisional Court Agreement of the International Settlement, reorganized and established. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs formally notified the British, American, French, Dutch, Norwegian, and Brazilian ministers on May 8, 1929. On October 31, a response was received from the Dutch minister, Odencrantz, representing the relevant countries. On November 19, 1929, a meeting was formally held in Nanjing, and it was signed on February 27, 1930. It came into effect on April 1 of that year, with a validity period of three years. Upon expiration, it could be extended for three years with the consent of both parties. The entire agreement consists of ten articles and eight annexes. Both parties also appointed two permanent representatives in accordance with Article 9 of the agreement as responsible personnel for interpreting the agreement in case of issues. Now that the agreement has been proposed for revision by our side, it will expire on March 31 of next year.

The British-Owned Bus Workers' Strike in the International Settlement Takes a Serious Turn 144

The Company Refuses to Negotiate with the Workers

White Russian Drivers and Passengers Injured

After the workers of the British-owned buses in the International Settlement went on strike, the company refused to negotiate and implemented the hiring of new workers. The strike committee issued a mobilization order, expelling White Russians, leading to disturbances yesterday. Several White Russians were injured, and passengers were affected, with the situation being very serious. The police received orders to step up precautions. Details are as follows:

Refusal to Negotiate 145

Based on the resolution of the mass meeting, the strike committee sent four worker representatives to the company on Kang Nao Road (Connaught Road) yesterday for direct negotiations, requesting: (1) reinstatement of those who were fired, and no more workers to be fired in the future; (2) a wage increase to forty yuan across the board, with an annual increase of three yuan thereafter, and wages to be paid during the strike period; (3) restoration of the copper coin bonus, issued according to the original standards; (4) uniform replacement of new cards, replaced every six months thereafter. Xiao Da, the factory's chief in charge of both factory and car affairs, refused to meet them, stating that the company had already announced the complete dismissal of those on strike, making negotiation impossible.

Hiring New Workers 146

The British-owned China General Omnibus

Page 14

Company, in order to restore public bus services on various routes, Factory Director and Chief of Car Affairs Xiao Da specially dispatched Associate Pi Ya to directly recruit new workers from the China Vocational Introduction Agency. Therefore, only twenty-five new workers were recruited. At 10 AM yesterday, the company specially dispatched a dedicated vehicle, driven by Associate Pi Ya, to Nanjing Road Bund to transport them to the company on Kang Nao Road. The strike committee believed that the company's refusal to negotiate and its strong attitude were unreasonable and allowed the striking workers to take direct action, issuing an order to expel White Russians who violated strike discipline. At the same time, a declaration was issued, notifying Chinese passengers to avoid accidental impacts. They considered that the operation of public buses would affect the future of the strike and implemented the work of stopping the buses. A Mr. Liu, a passenger wearing a Western suit, had strong acid splashed on his eyes. A Mr. Mou, dressed in Chinese clothing, had strong acid splashed on the back of his head. At the same time, striking workers assaulted Russians on Route 1, Route 2, and Route 9 buses. Seven White Russians, including Bi Baifu, Liji Fu, Dakonuo Fu, and Yin Qi Yinji, were assaulted. Passengers Mr. Liu and Mr. Mou were also injured.

Company Statement 149

Yesterday, due to striking workers assaulting Russians and affecting passengers, the British-owned China General Omnibus Company suspended service on Route 6, from the Ti Lan Qiao to the Bazi Chang bus route, starting at 1 PM. The company sent the assaulted White Russians to the hospital and will fully bear all losses and medical expenses for the innocent passengers affected.

Armed Protection 150

In addition, Mr. Qiang Tela, the Deputy Chief of Car Affairs of the company, specially rushed back to Shanghai from Japan due to the workers' strike and is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at 9 AM today.

Measures for Handling Mail from the Three Northeastern Provinces by the Local Postal Bureau 165

The Shanghai Postal Administration has made corrections regarding the measures for handling mail from the Three Northeastern Provinces. Yesterday, Bureau Edict No. 1629 was issued, stating: "For the purpose of notifying matters, the suspension of postal services in the Three Northeastern Provinces and the measures for mail from the Three Northeastern Provinces were previously notified in Bureau Edicts No. 1602, No. 1606, and No. 1612. Now, the order from the General Post Office is open, and the supplementary measures for mail from the Three Northeastern Provinces are detailed below. All are to be followed and implemented: (1) All types of imported mail originating from the Three Northeastern Provinces (excluding the South Manchurian Railway Zone) and forwarded through Dalian or other foreign exchange bureaus, affixed with (1) "Manchukuo" postage stamps, (2) Japanese ordinary postage stamps, or (3) Republic of China postage stamps, and canceled with various styles of Japanese chops (including those with the year 32 chop), shall be regarded as mail with insufficient postage and charged double the postage. If encountering sealed general packages, they shall be rejected. However, mail affixed with uncanceled Republic of China postage stamps, or mail genuinely originating from the Kwantung Leased Territory and affixed with Japanese postage stamps, shall still be treated as mail with sufficient postage. All mail originating from the South Manchurian Railway Zone (excluding the Kwantung Leased Territory), if affixed with Japanese ordinary postage stamps, shall be treated as underpaid, but only the domestic postage rate shall be charged. (2) Export mail: A. All mail addressed to various places in the Three Northeastern Provinces (excluding the South Manchurian Railway Zone and the Kwantung Leased Territory) shall not be accepted. If dropped into mailboxes, it shall be immediately returned to the sender or sent to the undeliverable mail office. B. All export mail going to the Kwantung Leased Territory or the South Manchurian Railway Zone shall be accepted and forwarded through Dalian as usual (see Annex No. 5 to the Sino-Japanese Postal Agreement No. 545 in the Foreign Language Circular). C. All export mail going to Korea shall be forwarded through Dalian or Japan to the destination as usual. D. All export mail going to the Asian part of Russia shall be handed over to direct steamships and forwarded via Shanghai and Vladivostok. Do not forward it through Japan. E. All export mail going to European countries and the European part of Russia, even if specifying transshipment via Japan or Siberia, shall still be rerouted by sea, using the fastest steamships via the Suez Canal or the Pacific Ocean. In short, regarding the sealing and forwarding methods for mail formerly transshipped via Siberia or the Three Northeastern Provinces (excluding the South Manchurian Railway Zone and the Kwantung Leased Territory), unless further instructions are given in the future, Japan shall not be used as a transshipment bureau for such mail. If various bureaus receive various types of letters from overseas, whether ordinary, registered, or insured, originally destined for various places in the Three Northeastern Provinces (excluding the South Manchurian Railway Zone and the Kwantung Leased Territory), they shall be stamped with "Postal Services Suspended in the Three Northeastern Provinces, Return to Sender" and returned to the original sending bureau. Also, if various bureaus receive imported international ordinary insurance or cash-on-delivery parcels originally intended for the Three Northeastern Provinces, they shall be handled according to the following methods: All parcels sent from the United States shall be immediately returned to the original sending bureau through the usual exchange bureau, and the exchange bureau shall choose the cheapest freight rate and postal route for their return. If sent from Europe, they shall first consult the original sending bureau and solicit the sender's opinion before returning them. If the sender requests return, our exchange bureau shall return them to the original sending bureau, but careful consideration must be given to choosing the cheapest postal route (the Greater Shanghai Route). Also, for mail or parcels concerning places in the Three Northeastern Provinces other than the Kwantung Leased Territory or the South Manchurian Railway Zone, the mail or parcels shall be returned to the sender regardless of whether the postage stamps are canceled or not, even if the mail or parcels have not left the original sending bureau. It should be noted that the withdrawal of our Chinese postal service from the Three Northeastern Provinces is a matter of necessity due to force majeure and should be handled according to the established precedent of force majeure." Upon receiving this, all are to comply and implement accordingly. This edict is issued by Postal Director Zha Pei, Lin.
